et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	And if it is not healed, or the incision is not completed throughout, because the patient does not wish to rest, or due to the bleeding out, then it is necessary that you fill the wound with wet cotton in a corrosive ointment;
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	And let it be as long as it can chew while removing and replacing it, then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	removing abscesses from the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	Abscesses that occur in the armpits are methods of hard scrofula or those with knots, and if there are any containing moisture.

de la routure de l’artere	regarding the rupture of an artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is punctured, and the skin is sewn where it was cut off, many times there are abscesses. And similarly this happens with an inflamed vein and abscess.

et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens .i. estraignement; et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	And when you feel it with your fingers, if you feel resistance; and when it's due to the vein, there is often an outward swelling;

des apostemes des ners	from abscesses of nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, as with abscesses in the artery and vein, there are nerve abscesses when they are inflamed, or due to too much work, and similar conditions.

des grosses boces pendans	of large breasts hanging down

quant li boude ist fuer	When it comes to the eye,
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	The appearance of the eye results from a fire wound or cut on the nose, and it can occur anywhere on the body, especially in other joints like hands. dou chancre	and gangrene
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer; et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement; et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	We have discussed in the division the appearances of gangrene and how to treat it with medicines, and how to avoid iron treatment. We will say that gangrene can occur anywhere in the body where it is possible to excise it, such as gangrene occurring around the breasts, in cooking, and in similar locations. You should remove all of it when it first appears; however, if a gangrenous lesion becomes large and old, it should not be treated near it because I have never known anyone to recover from it before me; no one has ever recovered from such lesions in front of me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the operation is within you where it can be excised as we have said, such that you cleanse the patient of black bile; then let the surgeon operate if there's evident swelling, then cut open the diseased area. That means a clean place to make an incision for the operation; then wash off your clamps or gangrene, and hair everywhere, and bone everywhere without leaving anything; and let all bleeding be stopped properly, and thoroughly dry the wound with your hand or any substance, and if it bleeds after healing in opposition to the incision of an artery or vein, cauterize until the wound is fully healed; then treat again until it becomes healthy.
de ydropisie	Of cautery by fire, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces .ij. semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	We have discussed the symptoms of erysipelas in the division, and how an assembly of water is formed, and the signs for each symptom, and the treatment done by medicine, and that which is treated by metal: these are clear; and should one not use metal in these four symptoms: this means, peritonitis and erysipelas, because it is a deadly thing; thus when you are treating this erysipelas symptom called 'flares' with medicine, and the treatment doesn't help, if you notice that the patient's health is weak, or they have another disease other than erysipelas, such as stomach solution and similar things; then do not touch metal, because there's a doubt; and if you see the patient very green in coloration, and they only have erysipelas disease and are neither too old nor too young, then you should proceed to operate:

fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue. de l’estopement de la verge	Regarding the constriction of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	No child is born without hairs on the penis, or if the hairs are small, or not in their place. If it suits to pierce both .i. (a unit of measurement) very thin spots according to this form: then put one .i. (again referring to a unit of measurement) small hair from plant material, and tie and keep it like this for .iij. (three) or iiij. (four) days. Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut. de la piere	from the stone

Je ai ja ce proveit ensi. I have already proven this method effectively.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron tree according to this shape and have it pierced with three pegs on one prong.
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Then take one thread and tie the loop around the rod near the stone so that it cannot return to the bladder; then drive the iron tree into the rod gently until it reaches the stone; and turn the iron tree in your hand near the stone gradually, until you can pierce the stone from the other side; if urine comes quickly, then press your hand on what remains of the stone inside the rod. et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez. de la piere des femmes	From the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It happens that a stone becomes enmeshed in women, and if it occurs once, then the treatment is difficult, and forbidden for three reasons: one is perhaps that the woman is virginal; and the second reason is that we cannot find a woman who knows how to protect herself from looking at men, even when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. de hernie carnouse	Of fatty hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non. de erratique	Regarding the erratic one
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Erratic refers to when the nature of the woman is not understood completely, or when there are deficiencies that are minor; it is naturally occurring by birth, or accidental due to disease that has come about. et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	they are always Persian fistulas; and they are recognized by those who experience an expulsion or windiness when the patient expels something, and sometimes in their movement from one area to another.

And for those fistulas that pierce up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis; and extend up to the knee joint, and up to the base of the testicle.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows if the fistula persists at the root, and not persisting:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and mark it when you press your index finger or root, and insert a fine needle or spider's leg in the fistula if there is no winding.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has winding, you should insert a fine tentacle or one of horsehair, as long as you feel the tentacle or hair at your index finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you don't feel it, and there's no sign of drainage or windiness nor smell, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	you'll know that it doesn't puncture; then hurry to treat.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends up to the bladder or up to where urine is conducted, if it jumps with urine, and cannot be sealed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it passes only up to the ankle joint, then there is the vein leading up to the top;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no tortuosity and the pain's origin is not inside, then it means that there's a swelling beneath, and it doesn't benefit from medicine or simply through application of ointment;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian fistulas there is no remedy but work and the vanity of those who interfere, showing their foolishness.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In the one that's neither Persian nor old, there is hope for healing through iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And it is when the body lies in your hands on its back; and lift its legs up to its hips, and incline its hips towards its abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then use an arachnid's tentacle, or that of a snail if there are twists, until you know where the tentacle comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels pain in the depth of their body, it is necessary that you press your index finger there.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	You will then feel that the tentacle has penetrated; and find it out where you sense between your index finger either a softness or the bone, then you know it is deep.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If there's no movement in that place, one cannot measure it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One must know though that one can indeed heal many, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and in assisting with this, if one is to apply the delicate cautery according to the width of the fistula, as has been explained previously;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and immerse it completely hot in the fistula until it reaches the base; and perform this twice or three times, as long as you know that these heated particles are burned away, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat with wet swabs soaked in butter until the heated particles are expelled, then apply ointment that hardens and binds.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is thus healed, that's good. If not, then there can't be another way to heal it;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if you try to pass it through and only pierce up to the base or foundation, then in between your finger and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or fat, and you see the fistula at that spot where the covering meets the skin.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If you remove through the beginning of the fistula and push until before the tent, then after that apply the cautery, as far as it reaches to the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	And you will remove the tent, and it will drain. Then cleanse those fatty tissues that resemble a bird's feather, making sure not to leave any remnants.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if you can't see it, cut between yourself and the wound, then apply either a fire cautery or an ointment in its place.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For the fire cauterizations combine two things: that is to say, the application of these charred substances and the bleeding out and drying off from moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then remove wet bandages with butter or ground things until the blood flows out, and let the burned substances finish in the fire.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with bindings soaked in hard wax, and use dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it has been restored, if it is healed, and does not return again.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes up just to the bottom edge, and is far from the body, then you should press your finger or the bottom part of it, and inquire about this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	And if you feel the membrane and it is inside two layers or if there's pus or scabs present, close to piercing, should only find a path of infection and hope; through the application of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you apply cautery as we have said, or you stop it just before the bottom, or if you can, place a needle and a cure like the first;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too far forward, that you might grasp the substance that supports the foundation, and bring about the evacuations by your own willing action;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then apply the cautery, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is clean, or you remove that covering and cleanse it since it has been separated from the foundation, either by accident or with another tool.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then remove with your hand the pus in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then try to heal the wound, and delay the pus flow in the lower part of the base: if it is lighter for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And always drain abscesses in this way: and when you squeeze the tentacle into the abscess, and it is close to the base of the skin below,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tentacle piercing at the head according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And tie two twisted threads together, and keep the thread taut within the duct until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is Persian in the margin beneath the foundation within, then extract the thread from that twisted one, just as you would bend your finger or base.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and pull the head of the thread, and join the two shoulders together, and tie one to the other, and let it be for an inch or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it each time, until the threads reach these points that are between the two and meet;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it has healed and is clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If a fistula does not puncture, make it puncture in all the ways that you can, provided it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not proper to make a covering for it when it is too deep, and then treat it as we have said, until it is clean.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spicular pus-filled fistula that one makes for a fistula is hard and from another, part and cutting it.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand no, because what we do not handle, we should also not handle, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of embolisms
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Emboli can be in two ways: either they are inside the vessel, like bits of resin, and there are both small and large ones, and they cause blood clotting,
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And if there is one or more of them, and are outside the vessel wall and at the base of the vessel's wall; but those that are outwards have little moisture,
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And also even just a little bit of yellow water or even just a little blood, and has the color of a corpse;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And for those treated internally within the foundation, you instruct the patient to take medicine that causes perspiration until the foundations are exhausted, and this becomes evident through their sweat and they reveal themselves.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you need to, twist it with pliers, or hold onto your finger, then apply pressure on its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the nail does not stay because of its moisture, take it with thread, or cotton, or a piece of leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And remove them with your hands, then clean them, and apply some hot powders on them that are used in the fire cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you might cauterize them as described or according to the cautery chapter, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot come out, you might cauterize the patient for a bowel obstruction that is sharp and rough to wash out what is in the foundation, so it can come out freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	if the patients cannot pass their stool, and if there are threads in the foundation, then the treatment should be light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should grasp them with your thumb or forceps and extract them, then treat if according to what we have said, until they are healed, and they fear the metal incision.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you suture according to this manner: take one twisted thread and place it in a needle, then pull the thread upwards and make the needle pierce from another side, and turn both ends of the threads around the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And if it is broad; and tie the thread in a knot, then tie the thread itself, remove the needle, and do so for all others, and leave one to cover excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the wound one moistened pad in oil of rose or poultice, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let them until they reach full length, and when they are fallen off, apply oil treatments and other remedies, as long as it remains healthy.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	do the drying by fire or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there has been drying from ashes in the intestines, and due to the nature's compulsion, and when the disease is old and medicine no longer helps.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary for you to place at the tip of a thorn or on your nail the skin above it, which should not be left wet;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then apply the treatment until it is firm as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot harden, start rasping more forcefully than before, until some healing occurs, and leave it burnt.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then continue the treatment until it is healed.
dou fremit	A tremor
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Antlworms is a false small appearance before the body, and goes most around it.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And whenever blood flows to the heart, and one feels it also like death due to trembling, and comes throughout the body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a rod from a goose feather or a strong vulture feather, and place this rod on the trembling, until the red circles eliminate the trembling completely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all of the cane until you capture the entire tremble and put it forward, and eradicate the tremble from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see something like this on an arachnid or iron in this form, and make it slender from underneath and draw it upwards:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Don't pierce it though, but hold it at the two ends and squeeze it. And if you see something like this, cauterize the tremble in front or chapter of the cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the shape of a bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	No silver paste or copper paste is ever made, or melted spider or wax; and no small or large instrument is ever made according to the one it's being applied to.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when dealing with the treatment of children and those who are weak and in pain, they need small things.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the small or large paste is like this, or the stomachs are bound in this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	And it allows the stomachs to be bound in this way, as you see, and the shoulder is pierced within; and there are two parts on one side and one part on the other side.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And if it is the stomach where you place medicines from a beast's bladder or parchment, and pierce it completely through with tiny pieces.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And have between each piece one inch of space, then insert one strong thread in these pieces, winding it through ten times or around the entire circumference, and join the stomach as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medicine is inside, seal it with a strong thread in front of the tool, then cauterize; and this forms like a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And ensure the medicine is neither too hot nor too cold, and grease the edge of the cauterizer with oil or yolk, or something similar, then gently insert it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the surgeon operates with both his hands together, as long as he can see it clearly, then removes the bladder stone, and lifts the patient's legs onto the operating surface.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine is supposed to come out, let it come as much as you can; and if he sleeps through a whole night, then it's more effective aid.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you administer castor oil for the ailment of belly evacuation, and the medicine is meant to quickly come out, then repeat it until he feels better.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if there's bleeding from the anus or its base, or an abscess, then use a castor oil as fine as one for half a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And it is this form beneath the subtle lymph node where the skin is constrained:
des plaies	Of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have discussed the treatment of wounds in the section on healing; now we will discuss hand care and medicine according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are varied depending on how they are made, and where they are made in the body, and why they were caused.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The ways wounds are made include through the impact of stones, and cuts from swords and knives, or from spears or clubs or hammers, or by similar means.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	that are made according to the anatomy of the body, such as wounds that occur on the neck, or head, or chest, or belly, or liver, and similar parts;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, starting with simple head wounds since their description will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head or face, and if the bone is not broken, take care whether it's due to stone or similar things, and all the skin has been torn away and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you slightly suspect an abscess in the middle: if there is a little blood from the wound immediately after it was injured, and then heal with the cephalic method; or if not, heal against the part affected.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And when the patient's body is filled with wine and heavy meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if they do not want to recover, let them reduce their meat intake, and abstain from drinking wine or eating meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place a dressing on the wound, if there are abscesses present, use moistened cotton in oil rosewater only, or in vinegar.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there are no abscesses present, place something on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and has not moved due to air, use a powder that I will mention later;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if they have healed, then apply certain ointments until they are clean.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a tailor's cut and similar injuries, and the lips cannot be joined together by stitching, then join them through sewing, as I will say for wounds in the belly, with stitches.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound exposes the bone and is deep, holding only to a small part if stopped; then treat the wound with medicine and restore hard tissue in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And instruct the patient to consume large meats, such as testicles and cooked wheat, like chickens, and similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or smell flesh rotting, and it doesn't touch the bone, then cut out the whole rotten part, flush with water, then treat it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is blood flowing in the wound or vein, without stoppage, and it cannot be stemmed by medicine, then you must tie the artery, and if you find that it has been dislocated, then fasten it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, then apply cautery.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light: and you put this powder which seals in such a way that when the fire touches it, it stops moving.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way to make this powder is as follows: take a part of incense; dragon's blood .ii parts; fresh garlic .iii parts, and finely ground powder,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, press it firmly until it dries well and joins completely with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then cover it well, and leave it without letting it loosen, if it doesn't swell; for the medicine should not be removed until it heals.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And never do this with charcoal alone, when one doesn't have the incense or the dragon's blood oil, but only that the surgeon has treated the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the surgeon has treated the wound, in the same manner, do not put this powder anywhere else;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some prepared bandages or on oats flour mixed with water and honey until it starts to flow;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue with other treatments until the wound heals.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if bone-breaking comes along with the wound, and it's small, then use delicate probes to treat it;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about the breaks of the head later.
de la plaie dou col	from the wound in the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This wound occurs in the neck and is simple, if there's no difference between this and those of the head, but if it affects the throat or the artery, then that makes a difference.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the nerves, if there is no other thing than to leave the treatment alone, and not to put any restraining thing, because it harms the nerves and causes them to recede;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not put anything cold on the wound, because the substance of nerves is cold, and their continuity here is with the brain, which is the highest member;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but use warm medicine instead, such as rose water washed with soft water, and also wash the cloth in soft water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other herbal remedies in this manner, and moist applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, sew it with bandages as long as it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and covered with hair and full of pus, pierce them or do so lower down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and bleeding occurs, causing it, open it, set it right, and burn it as necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the throat or ribs are cut, or the passage is disturbed, through which meat travels,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if you apply heat to the throat bone, and do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then allow the swelling to subside, and let it be for some days, then treat with dried ointments until it heals;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if there is a mark on the bone from the wound, you should remove it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bits of bone, you might chip them out thoroughly, and leave those that you cannot remove until the wound heals,
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And when it has drained and healed, then its nature will show.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I've mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there are bones in the wound and it has an abscess, treat it as I have said in my chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	from the wound of a spear or a knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's due to a spear or knife, and the wound is deep, when you observe that there's wind flow out of the wound instead of air: know then that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it's not deep and all its blood is fresh, then don't put powder there at first hour or bind it without the blood moving properly to the extremities.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and revive the heart, and keep the patient calm;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply a drawing ointment, and bind it twice a day;.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	And if you do not have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	Let the patient rest on the wound for 3 days, or 4, or more if needed;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	If there is no pain, nor bad trembling of the heart, nor sudden movements;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good signs, know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat with remedies and other treatments until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal and grow, know that there will be a sinus; treat as you should for such cases.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision and it's simple or worse, or on the back, treat according to who is present.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it's large, stitch it up; and if it's small, use powder; and if it is close to the bone, or has penetrated bones, then clean the wound and remove any foreign objects inside.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not evacuated, let the wound fester, if it lightens the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And concerning other wounds or other parts, we have made our judgements as we said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	from the rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the abdomen are large, medium-sized, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound jumps out an organ of the intestines or of the bowel cavities, which causes an invasion by them.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And sewing it up is more troublesome; indeed, there is nothing that matches a small wound better than a large one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Thus, when we place the intestines back in, if they are not placed carefully one by one;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	Because the intestines swell almost immediately upon feeling cold, hence they cannot be forced further into their original positions.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And for this reason you must clean the wound, for this reason we move to reposition the intestines in their place like the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that there are four ways of stomach rupture:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common incisions occur in the abdominal incision,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the other incisions for injuries to the body and two other specific incisions are common with other injuries;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And still they are more suitable with the stitches under the belly, and I will say each one and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and there's nothing of the intestine exposed,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and for the matter of replacing it, one can do this in two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the size of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	Because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Soak a sponge or two parts of a towel in water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in boiling water with quina and thorn needles,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And let the intestines grow until they are cut off;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this has been done with the wine restraining and medicating, it should relieve swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling leave, moisten the intestines with water or broth that has been cooked and seasoned.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because through this, the entry allows for little passage of substances;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, they make a small cut with the tool from which one removes the hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to apply heat to the wound,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	That we should not cut it without great necessity or avoid it;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument to open it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	If you cut inside the bend and not outward, and see this form:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you reset it according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the strength, for this is valuable movement.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide, and it's located on the side of the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	It is necessary for you to treat the patient on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and place their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it's located on the side of the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	Place the head and tail higher than the other parts.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	And also if there is a rupture in the belly at one of the two sides.
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	And place your understanding such that the severed part be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, it is to administer what I say about large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	Treat small wounds with what you are equipped for,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then hold them in your hands, minister remedies that heal all the rupture to their hand,
et assemble les levres;	and bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common way of sewing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and it involves taking one or more needles, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave at the edge of the wound enough space for two fingers, and insert one needle with plenty of thick thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce both ends of the leather with both needles from the skin,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which lies within the skin as long as you pierce that part of it,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and connect together the two principal openings of the four into one;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then pass a double thread through an eyelet in each of these two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	and stitch the two edges of the wound together.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And then leave one dot of space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then sew with the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this according to what you need to do with the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And use needles of medium size, between fine and large ones,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because the very fine needles cut all the flesh, and those that are too large do not fit well to enter:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	for this reason they should be of medium size;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not good to have the needles sticking out too much from the flesh and the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	They do not cut and bleed the wound before the stitch;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then remove the needles from the wounds so that they do not irritate the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and I place tents or cloths over the insertion sites of the needles to keep them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is stitched.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because one uses a needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it involves sewing together the two layers of leather and the two layers of stuffing onto one needle with one strong thread in the middle;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced these joints all together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then pull the needle at the part where you started, in the way one sews linen;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave a space between each stitch as big as a small coin;
ceste costure sevent li home,	these stitches should be even.
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	And here I am to heal a wound where once there was a large lump or belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which had been made by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm in size,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and contained the intestines well up to two palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And there was a wound between the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I brought back his intestines, and it had been xxix hours since it occurred.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound healed up to fifteen days, I treated it, and he was well.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And I would not treat it with ointment, for I was in the first year where one could not find any, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And I would change the cloth covering the wound two times a day, and wash it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper methods of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and at first from outside to inside until it reaches there;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When she has pierced through to the heart directly on the direct line, if it hits the head of the syphilitic or causes chest pain, you have punctured the needle.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	And make her pierce from another side starting from inside until it reaches this point outward;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And the understanding of this stitch is such that you sew it in the same way as the mink does with its fur,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And let the siphac once on one side, and then take it up from the other, until the stitch is fully completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of sewing up wounds, as Galen truly explained,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	It is just like how everyone does it, uniting the two parts in their natural position,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	And they press one part of the wound with its edge against another part, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Insert a needle or point of the wound near the mouth, and make a hole only on the surface.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	And let both of these shoulder heads grow.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outer part until inside.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	like both shoulder heads;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both from the outer part until inside, using two other shoulder heads that are on the opposite side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the way to sew and the most common method.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galien said these words, and no one testifies to them,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One should sew the belly with two needles, or if there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one should place one needle on one side and the other on the other side, like those who sew tinned items;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the rupture is within the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	then the stitching is more painful than in other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments on wounds are similar to those for other types of wound:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you find the fresh wound with all its blood, as if the art has made it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	If it is placed back in the intestine, and at the cut; then place above the stimulating powder,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	And if it has burned it, so apply any present salve until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And sew the thread, and let them fuse the cuticle, and make the incision heal;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as usual, until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you don't have medicine, place it above, as soon as it begins to drip oil,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it twice a day until it becomes healthy.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you don't need any other medicines in various preparations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound might spread to the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	If you need to moisten wool lightly in oil of warmed heat, or in rose-scented oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and put it inside the joints, and over the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or gangrene in the bowels, and this happens repeatedly,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if you use black wine enemas, and especially if the gangrene has spread up to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And insert inside, and know that when it's large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called 'young' cannot be healed when it is injured,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And this is due to the positioning of the veins and because of the subtlety of the entire body, and its alignment with its nature towards nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the lump from the wound jumps up, then reset it as with the intestine while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it's old and turned brown or black, then you should tie the black area, so that no blood flows there,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the tie,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place both shoulders down to the area over the wound until beyond it for ease of extraction when the sockets move, and let the wound heal.
de la routure dou boueil	of the rupture of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are ruptured, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in any way,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I see that some were pierced by a spear in their belly;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	And there was a wound on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and became stenosed and turned into a fistula, causing malabsorption and gas production;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I performed the treatment according to my ability, and continued refining it until it was effective, ensuring proper closure of the wound.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it properly healed, I worried that there might be problems with the patient's stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And there was no harm, but it remained in better conditions, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And it was said by some experimenters that when there is a small injury in the intestine, it should be treated like this:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large bulbs (of garlic), then join the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the garlic has opened its mouth, place it on the two edges,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if she forces her mouth up;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then he holds the head, and this is maintained if it cannot be released,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then applies another rub to in that manner as before, until the wound has been thoroughly rubbed;
et cout la plaie.	and close the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those who become hot in the intestine, and do not cause any harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can bind the intestine with a fine thread that is cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in such a manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestine thread so that most of it has been dried,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	And then to the head of this thread .i., a fine linen thread twisted,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then thread the needle with the thread and sew through the intestine, then remove it at the incision;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this way of sewing like a seam is only according to the path of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and broad, especially when it's in one of the intestinal loops, if there's no child or health, it requires subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	regarding a fistula or if it be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that any wound or abscess, as it matures, is universally called "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and likewise when it is sealed and begins to heal.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the true swelling that lasts and is white, or where one does not feel pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	It is also as hairy as the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And not once in clear white flesh, and another time thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Not always little, and sometimes enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken about the division of wounds in that section; that any wound that is not healed and has no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	This comes from none of the eight reasons:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	it is to say, due to the smallness of blood or pus;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its maleficence;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh inside and against the lips that prevents new flesh from forming;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	There's too much blood;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	the lungs are inflamed, and the matter is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine used in treatment isn't good;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption resembles pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	For by the nature of the area being late in digestion, and delayed healing, and flees naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	for there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicines in this division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	It is necessary that I inform you about the treatment of fistulas which is performed by manual labor.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in all limbs of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that originate from large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the stomach, or in the intestine, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spinal column of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And if this comes to possess the main member's property, and they resemble it.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are in this manner cause difficulty with healing, and there is nothing else but labor, and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is no fistula that does not end up at the place I have mentioned, and you have begun the treatment,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you will know it, take a spider's web or iron wire, if the fistula is straight, try to insert it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	And if the fistula is twisted, seek out with a subtle probe to uncurl it,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	for the probe bends and moves along in the twist;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula has no branches and you cannot find it well by trying with probes,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	then irrigate it through one of its branches,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	because moisture can travel from one place to another, and gets purified;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then feel it carefully with your hand, so you know if there is bone or nerve, and check the hair around it.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient precisely about the pain they feel when your hand presses on it, and where in their body does that pain occur;
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and when you truly understand the location of her/his pain and whether it is far from a joint, or a nerve, or an artery or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	In any of the limbs that I have told you about, if the application follows what I have told you,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and expose the bone of the patient and the rotten carcass that is within;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then continue the treatment until it heals,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	and if the fistula is deeply and correctly opened, it is fitting that you seal it completely as much as possible.
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then I place moistened bandages in medicine water, and let them soak up to the tip of the fistula.
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine dissolves what has remained at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then I apply clean bandages until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if it doesn't heal through this method, then cauterize it as we have explained,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is rotten from the ulcer, then operate it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve is being pressed or affecting main limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed, and there's decay and darkness, then treat it until the decay has been completely removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cleanse the wound with various remedies until it heals properly;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	If it's not healed, and if you move it back as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	Know that you haven't gone far enough until the sound stops:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	Search deeply and thoroughly until you reach the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all the decay; then return to its original place.
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it's like this healthy, then indeed it is well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	But if not so, know that the corruption has spread too far, that you cannot restore it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other way than to leave it to nature;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there's just a small corroded bone, and you can extract it with forceps,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if you extract with an instrument suitable for this,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many, treat them all, don't leave any;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and should moisture oppose this and there be neither error nor fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	if you have bone and moisture along with heat, and free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, then apply something to the wound that promotes healing,
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it stay until the joints are softened inside the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	then the bones will then come out more easily;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it's a large bone, like from the thigh or leg,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	if you remove them only until the blackness is entirely bone,
puis restoure la plaie;	then heal the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there's a large portion rotten, and it reaches up to the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	if it should be to cut right up to the decay and then heal it as long as it is joined together;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	And I will tell you of a case where a fistula occurred in someone's leg.
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	so that you may take this as an example and aid yourself in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young person of around thirty years old, who had pain in their leg due to an issue that came from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	The matter would travel to the leg and there formed a large abscess; there was no external cause for opening it.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	yet they opened them so wide that the abscesses were opened,
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and removed very little of the contents, and formed a tunnel, and there was much loss that all caused sweat and moisture from the body;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and many physicians treated the condition for two years, and there was no expert in the art of healing.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	until I arrived where I was called, and saw his leg and the medicines used to treat him,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And that which moves through the narrow parts with great force;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And his body would turn red as if in youth, and had a yellowish color.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I built a tent in one of these narrow parts, and then sought all the narrow parts,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that some came against each other from all sides of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I hurried then, and scraped one of the fractures until I revealed a part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and found it decayed and pierced, and the decay had reached inside to the bone;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I saw what appeared from the decayed bone, and thought there was no other decay, just the one I found;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	and began to treat the wound with medicine over a long period, but could not heal it;
